1a1(rgyud 'grel): bsdus pa'i rim pa'i bsgrub thabs bzhugs so// /
1b1(rgyud 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ piN TI kra ma sA d+ha na
1b2(rgyud 'grel): bod skad du/ bsdus pa'i rim pa'i bsgrub thabs
2a1(rgyud 'grel): 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo// 'jig rten gsum gyi spyod pa las grol mkha' dang mnyam
2a2(rgyud 'grel): rtogs dngos po kun gyi ngo bo nyid// dag rnam dben mchog zhi'i rang bzhin rnal 'byor pa rnams nyid kyis rtogs bya ba//
2a3(rgyud 'grel): rtogs par dka' zhing rnam par dpyad par dka' la rang gzhan rab phan khyab cing mtshan ma med// rgyal ba rnams sku bde
2b1(rgyud 'grel): mnyam med mnyam pa'i rnam par sku gcig la phyag 'tshal// dpal ldan 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi ni// mtha' drug don ni rtogs pa las// sems can kun la phan bskyed
2b2(rgyud 'grel): ba/ bsdus pa'i rim pa bdag gis bshad// rnam rtog bag chags nyes pa yis// 'gro ba gsum po rnam rmongs la// blo dang ldan pas legs bltas nas//
2b3(rgyud 'grel): de rnams rnal 'byor rgyud kyis sbyangs// 'dod pa lnga ni yongs spangs nas// dka' thub kyis kyang ma gdungs par// rnal 'byor rgyud kyi rjes 'brangs nas//
2b4(rgyud 'grel): bde bas byang chub bsgrub par bya// de yis 'dir ni sdom gnas 'di'i// rtag tu mi phyed rtul zhugs pas// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje yi// sgrub pa yang ni
3a1(rgyud 'grel): brtsas par bya// dgon pa chen po sa phyogs mchog/ me tog 'bras bu sogs pas brgyan// ri bo skye bos dben pa ru// dngos grub thams cad bsdus pa bsgrub/ 'jam pa'i stan la 'dug nas ni// sems dpa'i dkyil dkrungs legs
3a2(rgyud 'grel): gnas te// zhe sdang rdo rje'i ting 'dzin gnas// gnas bsrung ba ni brtsam par bya// 'bar ba'i 'od 'phro 'jigs par byed// nyi ma la gnas hUM las byung / g.yon brkyang ba yi gom pas gnas// khro bo bcu ni spro bar bya// phyogs bcu'i dkyil 'khor rtse mor ni// rim pa
3a3(rgyud 'grel): bzhin du bsam par bya// bgegs kun rnam par gzhig pa'i phyir// gnod mdzes bka' bsgo phur bus gdab// oM sum+b+ha ni sum+b+ha hUM/ gr-ih+Na gr-ih+Na hUM/ gr-ih+NA pa ya gr-ih+NA ba ya hUM/ A na ya ho/ \u0f7fb+ha ga wAn bid+yA rA dza hUM phaT/ 'di yis khro bo'i gzugs kyis ni//
3a4(rgyud 'grel): bgegs kyi dbang po kun bkug nas// blo dang ldan pas sbyor ba yis// cho ga bzhin du phur bus gdab// rdo rje bdud rtsi rgyal po che// ud dpal sngon po'i 'dab ltar ljang // 'bar phreng 'khrigs pa'i 'od ldan pa// rdo rje phur bu rnam par bsgom// lte ba'i
3a5(rgyud 'grel): phyogs nas smad kyi cha// rtse mo'i rnam byar rnam bsam zhing // stong ni khro bo'i dbyibs can te// zhal gsum phyag drug rnam par bsgom// 'og tu bgegs kyi tshogs bltas nas// de yi sngags ni legs brjod cing // bgegs kyi lus la mi g.yo
3a6(rgyud 'grel): bar// rdo rje phur bu nges par gdag/ oM g+ha g+he/ g+hA ta ya g+hA ta ya/ sarba duSh+TAM/ phaT phaT/ kI la ya kI la ya/ sarba pA bA na/ phaT phaT/ hUM hUM hU~M/ badz+ra kI la ya/ badz+ra d+ha ro adz+nyA pa ya ti/ sarba bi g+h+nAM/ kI ya bAka tsIt+ta badz+ra ki la ya/ hUM hUM hUM/ phaT/
3b1(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje tho ba phyag bsnams pa'i// gnod mdzes rgyal po rnam par bsam// rdo rje'i mtshan ma kun tu me// rnam par 'phro ba nges par bsgom// gdug pa bris pa phan tshun du// cho ga par gyur pa rnam par bsam// phyogs bcur phur busna btab nas ni// zlog
3b2(rgyud 'grel): dang steng yang byin brlabs nas// dam pa'i don du srid pa gsum// rang dngos med par bsgom par bya// dngos po med la sgom pa med// sgom pa sgom pa ma yin nyid// de ltar dngos po dngos med de// sgom pa dmigasu med pa'o// tshigs bcad 'di yis
3b3(rgyud 'grel): brtan g.yo yi// bdag nyid stong par bsgoms nas su// cho ga'i sbyor ba 'di yis ni// ye shes sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs// rnam pa'i khams kyi dbus gnas par// sa bon/ hUM gnyis yaM lngas byung // rdo rje gnyis dang yang dag ldan// rlung gi dkyil
3b4(rgyud 'grel): 'khor sgom par bya// sa bon hUM gnyis raM las byung // rdo rje gnyis dang yang dag ldan// me yi dkyil 'khor nyid kyang ni// de yi steng du rnam par bsam// sa bon hUM gnyis baM las byung // rdo rje gnyis dang yang dag ldan// chu yi dkyil 'khor nyid kyang ni//
3b5(rgyud 'grel): daM yi steng du rnam par bsgom// sa bon hUM gnyis li las byung // rdo rje gnyis dang yang dag ldan// sa yi dkyil 'khor nyid kyang ni// de yi steng du rnam par bsam// dkyil 'khor bzhi po yang dag bsdus// rdo rje sa yi dkyil 'khor la// der ni hUM yig las
3b6(rgyud 'grel): byung ba'i// gzhal yas khang pa rnam par bsgom// gru bzhi dang ni sgo bzhi dang // rta babs bzhi yis mdzes byas pa// srad bu bzhi dang yang dag ldan/ ka ba brgyad kyis nye bar mdzes// dra ba dra ba phyed pa dang // rdo rje nor bya zla phyed dang // sgo dang sgo khyud
4a1(rgyud 'grel): mtshams rnams su// rdo rje rin chen rnams kyis spras// bum pa kra ba rdo rje che// mnga' yab kyang ni logs can dang // ba dan dril bu mdzes byas pa/ rnga la ba sogs kyis rnam par brgyad// bdag nyid phyag rgyar ldan pa ni// zhal gsum phyag
4a2(rgyud 'grel): drug rnams pa la// in+d+ra ni la'i 'od mnyam pa// dkyil 'khor dbus su bsgom par bya// rnam snang mdzad dpal rin chen dang // 'od dpag med dang las kyi rgyal// zhal gsum phyag drug rnam par ni// shar la sogs pa'i phyogs su bsam// gti
4a3(rgyud 'grel): mug dga' sogs lha mo rnams// zhal gsum phyag drug rnam par ni// me yis phyogs su brtsams nas su// rim pa ji bzhin nges par dgod// de bzhin gzugs kyi rdo rje sogs// phyi yi mtshams ni rnam pa bzhir// reg bya rdo rje nyid kyang ni//
4a4(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje sems dpa' dang ldan gnas// byams pa sa yi snying po dag/ shAr gyi rnam bur dgod par bya// phyag na rdo rje mkha' snying po// brtul zhugs can gyis lho r+ya dgod// 'jig rten dbang phyug 'jam pa'i dbyangs// nub tu yang ni dgod par bya// spyi
4a5(rgyud 'grel): ba thams cad rnam sel dang // kun tu bzang po byang phyogs su// gshin rje gshed ni shar gyi sbyor// gzhan gyi mi thub lho phyogs su// nub phyogs su ni rta mgrin te// bdud rtsi 'khyil pa byang du'o// mi g.yo 'dod pa'i rgyal po dang // dbyug sngon
4a6(rgyud 'grel): dang ni stobs po che// shar gyi mtshams sogs nos brtsams te// ji lta ji bzhin bsgom par bya// gnod mdzes rgyal po khro bo che// 'og tu rab tu rnam par bsam// gtsug tor 'khor los bsgyur ba yang // de bzhin steng du rnam par bsgom// cho ga
4b1(rgyud 'grel): ji bzhin dkyil 'khor pa// de rnams lhags par mos bsams nas// slar yang kha sbyar sbyor ba yis// rang gi lus la de rnams gzhug/ lus kyi 'khor lor gtogs sangs rgyas// de ltar ji lta bzhin bsams nas// don dam pa yi 'khor lo
4b2(rgyud 'grel): I// de bzhin nyid du gzhug par bya// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs bsad na// dngos grub rab mchog thob par 'gyur// 'di don rdo rje phreng ba las// gsal bar ji bzhin rnam phye ste// gzugs phung gtogs pa mi long dang // sa khams
4b3(rgyud 'grel): mig gi dbang po dang // gzugs kyang lnga par 'gro ba ste// khro bo byams par yang dag ldan// tshor ba'i phung po mnyam nyid dang // chu khams rna ba'i dbang po dang // sgra yang lte par 'gro bar ste// khro bo gnyis dang yang dag ldan// 'du shes
4b4(rgyud 'grel): so sor rtog pa dang // byin za sna yi dbang po drang // dri yang lnga par 'gro ba ste// khro bo gnyis dang yang dag ldan// 'du byed bya ba grub pa dang // rlung khams lce yi dbang po dang // raM yang lnga par 'gro ba ste// khro bo gnyis dang yang dag ldan// steng
4b5(rgyud 'grel): 'og khro bo shin tu bcas// rang bzhin snang ba nyid kyang ni// rnam shes phung por kun nas 'gro/ rnam shes kyang ni 'od gsal du// mya nganA 'dus dang kun stong dang // chos kyi sku yang bshad pa yin// brtan par byed pa rgyu yi phyir// sngags 'di
4b6(rgyud 'grel): gsol bar brjod par bya/ oM shI n+ya ta dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+hA wa yang mgon te/ 'di ni don dam dkyil 'khor ste// snang ba med pa'i mtshan nyid do// don dam bden pa zhes kyang bya// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// 'od gsal bar ni rab
5a1(rgyud 'grel): zhugs nas// sngags kyi sku yi sbyor ba yis// lha yi dmigs pa'i don ched du// ldang ba yang ni bstan par bya// na mkha'i khams kyi dbus gnas par// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sngags pas yang ni de'i
5a2(rgyud 'grel): steng du// zla ba'i gzugs ni rnam par bsam// der yang pad ma 'dab brgyad pa// kha dog dmar po bsgom par bya// pad ma'i steng du sngags chen po// yi ge gsum yang bsam par bya// sngags dang pad ma nyi ma dag/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la
5a3(rgyud 'grel): zhugs pas// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs pa// byang chub sems su rnam par bsgom// rgyu dang mi rgyu thams cad ni// de nyid du ni rnam bsam zhing // brtan par bya ba'i don du ni// sngags 'di rab tu brjod par bya// oM d+harmA
5a4(rgyud 'grel): d+hA tu swa b+hA wa At+ma ko&haM/ de ltar rnal 'byor dmigs nas na// rjesu rnal 'byor brtsam par bya// rnal 'byor pa yi yog gsum yang // zla ba'i dbus su rnam par bsam// de nas yig gsum las byung dang // kun du zla ba dang mtshungs
5a5(rgyud 'grel): dkar// dang po'i mgon po bsam nas kyang // shin tu rnal 'byor yang dag brtsam// mi bskyod pa ni rjes zhugs pas// zhal gsum phyag drug 'bar ba dang // in+d+ra nI la'i 'od 'bar ba// rdo rje sems dpa' rnam par bsgom// rdo rje 'khor
5a6(rgyud 'grel): lo pad ma ni// de bzhin g.yas pa'i phyag tu bsam// dril bu rin chen ral gri ni// g.yon pa'i phyag tu bsam par bya// de nas phung po la sogs la// rnam snang li sogs gnod mdzes mthar// sa ben dgod pas dgod par bya// de nyid
5b1(rgyud 'grel): kyis ni rnam par bsgom// rnam snang mdzad kyi sa bon ni// kha dog dkar po yi ge oM// gzugs phung ngo bo nyid kyis ni// sngags shes pas ni spyi bor dgod// mgon po 'od dpag med kyi AH// 'du shes phung po'i bdag nyid can//
5b2(rgyud 'grel): mdog dmyur khA la bsam nas nI// ngag gi dbang phyug nyid thob bya// mi bskyod pa yi yi ge hUM// rab tu bzang ba'i mthing shun mdog/ rnam shes phung po'i ngo bo yi// sngags pas snying gar rnam par dgod// rin chen mgon po'i ye
5b3(rgyud 'grel): ge swA/ tshor ba'i phung po'i ngo bo yis// tshor ba dag pa'i rgyu nyid ni// kha dog ser po lte bar dgod// rkang pa gnyis lnga yi ge hA/ 'du byed phung po'i ngo bo dang // las kyi mgon po'i de nyid kyis// sngags pas kha dog ljang gur dgod//
5b4(rgyud 'grel): gti mug dga' sogs sngags pa yis// sa la sogs par rab tu zhugs// sa nyid gshe rA nyid dro ba dang // g.yo nyid der ni rim pa bzhin// th+liM mig tu bkod nas nI// sa yi snying po rnam par bsgom// oM yig rna ba dag la dgod//
5b5(rgyud 'grel): phyag na rdo rje bsgom par bya// oM yig sna la rnam bkod de// na mkha'i snying po rab tu bsgom// oM yig lce la bkod nas ni// 'jig rten dbang po brtag par bya// yid la yi ge hUM bsams nas// 'jam pa'i dbyangs ni rab tu bsgom// yi
5b6(rgyud 'grel): ge oM ni lus kun la'ang // bsgoms nas sgrib sel dran par bya// yi ge maM ni mgor bzhag nas// byams pa nyid du yongasu brtag/ tshigs kun la ni saM bkod de// kun tu bzang po bsgom par bya// lag pa g.yos par gshin rje gshed//
6a1(rgyud 'grel): g.yon par gzhan gyis mi thub pa// rta mgrin kha la bsam par bya// rdo rje la ni bdud rtsi 'khyil// dpung pa g.yas par mi g.yo ba// g.yon par 'dod pa'i rgyal po'o// pus mo g.yas par bsams pa ni/ dbyug pa sngon
6a2(rgyud 'grel): po cher 'bar gA/ pus mo g.yon par stobs po che// spyi bor gtsug tor 'khor los bsgyur// gnod mdzes rgyal po bsams pa ni// rkang pa gnyis la 'god par bya// phung po sogs la cho ga bzhin// sngags pas dgod par byas nas
6a3(rgyud 'grel): ni// sku yi dkyilo rdzogs gyur pas// de nas rnal 'byor chen po brtsam// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor yang dag rdzogs// mgo bo'i dbus su gnas par bsam// der ni yi ge oM dkar po// 'od zer lnga ni rab 'phro ba'o// de nas lha mo phyung nas ni//
6a4(rgyud 'grel): bdag po'i rab tu sbyor ba la// spyan ma rnam pa du ma ni// nam mkha' thams cad rab gang bsam// de nas sku yi rdo rje ni// nam mkha' gang bar bzhugs bsams te// de la dbus su bdag po ni// sum cu rtsa gnyis mtshan 'chang zhing // dpe byad brgya
6a5(rgyud 'grel): cus brgyan pa dang // bdag nyid mdun du gnas par bsam// de nas sngags pas tshigs bcad gnyis// brjod cing gsol ba gdab par bya// sangs rgyas sku 'dzin dpal dang ldan// rdo rje gsum dang mi phyed dngos// bdag la byin gyis brlabs gnas
6a6(rgyud 'grel): deng // sku yi rdo rje rnams kyis mdzod// phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// rdo rje gsum dang mi phyed dngos// bdag la byin gyis brlabs gnas dang // sku yi rdo rjes rnams kyis mdzod// spyan ma lhan cig mnyam ldan par// rtag pa yang
6b1(rgyud 'grel): ni rnam par bsam// de bcug nas ni phung po lnga// rab tu gang bar byin gyis brlag/ sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gang zhig/ phung po lnga yI rab tu rgyas// sangs rgyas sku yi ngo bo yis// bdag kyang de dang 'drar gyur cig/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta kA ya badz+ra swa b+hA wa at+ma ko/
6b2(rgyud 'grel): haM/ a yig kha dog dmar ldan pa// lce dbus pad mar gnas bsam ste// gos dkar zhes bya tshogs dang bcas// nam mkha'i khams rnams gang bar spro/ gsung gi rdo rje sngags pas yang // nam mkha' gang bar bzhugs pa la// de nas sngags
6b3(rgyud 'grel): pas tshigs bcad gnyis// brjod cing gsol ba gdab par bya// chos nyid gsung lam dpal dang ldan// rdo rje gsum dang mi phyed dngos// bdag la byin gyis brlabs nas deng // gsung gi rdo rje mdzad du gsol// phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs
6b4(rgyud 'grel): rgyas rnams// rdo rje gsum dang mi phyed dngos// bdag la byin gyis brlabs nas deng // gsung gi rdo rje rnams kyis mdzod// gos dkar mo ni lhan cig nyid// rang gi gtso bor yang dag ldan// lce la zhugs par rab bsams te// gsung gIs byin
6b5(rgyud 'grel): gyis brlab pa tsam// rdo rje chos kyi gsung gang zhig/ nges pa'i tshig ni phun sum tshogs// bdag gi tshig kyang de 'dra bar// chos 'dzin pa dang 'drar gyur cig/ oM sarba ta thA ga tA wA ke badz+ri swa b+hA wa at+ma ko haM/ sngags pas snying gar nyi ma yi//
6b6(rgyud 'grel): gzugs brnyan 'bar ba bsam bya ste// der ni mthing shun lta bu yi// hUM yig 'od zer lnga ldan dgod// de las lha mo mA ma ki/ tshogs dang bcas pa dbyung bar bya// de bzhin thugs kyi rdo rje bsgom// de la sngon bzhin gsol pa gdab// rdo
7a1(rgyud 'grel): rje thugs 'dzin dpal dang ldan// rdo rje gsum dang mi phyed dngos// bdag la byin gyis brlab gnas deng // thugs kyi rdo rjes mdzad du gsol// phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// rdo rje gsum dang mi phyed dngos// bdag la
7a2(rgyud 'grel): byin gyis brlab gnas deng // thugs kyi rdo rje rnams kyis mdzod// mA ma ki tshogs ma lus bya// thugs rdo rje dang yang dag ldan// snying gar yang ni bcug nas su// thugs kyi byin gyis brlab pa brtsam// kun tu bzang po'i thugs gang zhig/ gsang ba
7a3(rgyud 'grel): pa'i bdag blo ldan pa// bdag gi sems kyang de 'dra bar// rdo rje 'dzin dang 'drar gyur cig/ oM sarba ta thA gA ta tsit+ta badz+ra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko hUM/ de ltar rigs gsum dbye ba yis// so sor byin gyis brlabs nas ni// slar yang blo ldan sngags 'di yis//
7a4(rgyud 'grel): thams cad bdag nyid can du bya// oM sarba ta thA gra ta kA ya wAka tsit+ta badz+ra sa b+hA wa At+ma ko haM/ de ltar byin brlabs bdag nyid ni// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// mtshan ma drug dang yang dag ldan// dam tshig sems dpa' bsam
7a5(rgyud 'grel): par bya// snying ga'i dbus gnas phra mo ni// ye shes sems dpa' rnam par bsgom// ti 'dzin sems dpa' zhes bya ba// hUM yig de yi snying gar dgod// de ltar sems dpa' gsum bdag nyid// rnal 'byor chen por bdag bskyed nas//
7a6(rgyud 'grel): cho ga'i sbyor ba 'di yis ni// phyag brgya bsgrub pa brtsam par bya// rme sha can ni bdag nyid che'i// bu mo ut+pal mthing ka yi// 'dab ltar sngo sangs mig yangs ma// gzugs dang lang tshos brgyan brnyed nas// bsgrub pa po la gus mnyes gshin//
7b1(rgyud 'grel): legs par bslabs pa blangs nas su// oM yig mgo bor bsam par bya// aHyig dag gi lam la dgod// hU~M yig snying gar bsam bya zhing // lte bar sA dang rkang gnyis hA// spyan dang mA ma ki dang ni// de bzhin du ni gos dkar mo// sgrol ma yang ni
7b2(rgyud 'grel): sngags pa yi// sa la sogs pa rnam par dgod// lha mo gzugs kyi rdo rje sogs// de nyid la ni rnam bsam zhing // sa snying la sogs de rnams dang // snyoms par 'jug par bsgom par bya// lag g.yas rdo rje ro langs ma// g.yon par gzhan
7b3(rgyud 'grel): gyis mi thub ma// de yi khar ni khro gnyer ma// gsang bar ral pa gcig ma'o// gzhan yang dpung pa g.yas na yum// sna tshogs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs// g.yon du sna tshogs rin chen ma// phyag rgya rab tu bsgom par bya// pus mo g.yas la gnas
7b4(rgyud 'grel): par yang // sna tshogs pad+ma de bzhin gshegs// sna tshogs las ma g.yon pa la// spyi bor na mkha'i rdo rje ma// rkang pa gnyis kyi mtha' ru ni// sa 'dzin lha mo bzhag byas te// de ltar 'dus byas rnal 'byor pas// rdo rje ba dam yang dag brtsam//
7b5(rgyud 'grel): sngags pas hUM yig las skyes pa'i// rdo rje rtse mo lnga pa bsam// de bzhin de rtse dbus ma la// oM nI rnam par bsam par bya// de bzhin AHyig las byung ba'i// pad ma 'dab ma brgyad pa ni// 'od zer lnga yis khyab bsams la// de 'og
7b6(rgyud 'grel): bsgrub pa brtsam par bya// oM sarba ta thA ga ta a nu rA ga Na badz+ra swa b+hA wa at+ma ko ha~M/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i nga rgyal legs 'chang zhing // hUM gi glu yis kyang ni bskyod par bya// rang gi byang chub sems nyid byung ba'i tshe// 'di ltar phaT kyi gsang sngags des
8a1(rgyud 'grel): brjod bya// phyung ba'i mthar yang sngags pa yis// phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// byang chub sems kyis mchod bya zhing // sngags 'di gsal bar brjod par bya// oM sarba ta thA ga ta pU dza badz+ra swa b+hA wa
8a2(rgyud 'grel): at+ma ko hUM/ rang sngags yi ge las byung ba// rdo rje gsum gyis byin brlabs rang // pad ma'i dbus su bskyed nas ni// slar yang zhe sdang rdo rjer gyur// badz+ro d+haM ka sngags las byung ba'i// mi bskyod rdo rje can bsam pa// mgon po ral pa'i thor tshugs
8a3(rgyud 'grel): 'chang // mi bskyod pas ni dbu rgyan byas// mthing shun bzang po'i mdog ltar snang // sngo gnag dkar dang dmar ba'i zhal// rgyan rnams thams cad yongs su rdzogs// phyag drug par ni rnam par bsgom// rdo rje 'khor lo byed mu nI// g.yas pa'i
8a4(rgyud 'grel): phyag tu bsam bya zhing // dril bu yid bzhin nor bu dang // ral gri de yi g.yon du bsam// 'di ni thugs ka las byung nas// phyogs bcu rnams su gzigs nas ni/ sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul kun mdzad nas// chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor ste// zhe
8a5(rgyud 'grel): sdang rdo rje'i gzhi ru gnas pa'i// sems can ma lus ldegs sbyangs nas// slar byon rdo rje mgon po yi// spyan snga ru ni 'dug par gyur// sngags pas de ni bdag nyid kyi// snying gar rjes su zhugs par bsgom// snga ma'i gzugs ni yongs gyur
8a6(rgyud 'grel): nas// zhe sdang rdo rje'i gnas la bzhugs// in+d+ra ni la'i 'od 'bar ba// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dbus na zhugs// dpa' bo rang gi phyag rgyas 'khyud// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// drag po zhi dang 'dod chags che// zhal gsum gyis ni
8b1(rgyud 'grel): rnam mangs pa'o// zhe sdang rdo rjerje ting 'dzin gnas// dkyil 'khor thams cad spro bar bya// dza na dzi ka sngags las rdzogs pa'o// gtso bo rnam par snang mdzadad b+hang+ku/ snron ka'i zla zer ltar spang zhing // thor tshugs cod pan dag gis brgyan//
8b2(rgyud 'grel): dkar dang gnag dang dmar ba'i zhal// phyag drug zhi ba'i gzugs can dang // 'khor lo rdo rje pad ma dkar// g.yas pa rnams su rnam par bsam// dril bu yid bzhin nor ral gri// 'di yi g.yon du rnam par bsgom// de bzhin
8b3(rgyud 'grel): thugs ka las byung ste// gti mug spyod gnas skye dgu rnams// yang dag sbyangs te slar byon nas// shar phyogs kyi ni 'khor lor bzhugs// rat+na d+h+r-ika sngags las skyed pa'i// rin chen tog ni mkhas pas dbyung // zhi ba thor tshugs cod pan
8b4(rgyud 'grel): 'chang // mi bskyod pas ni dbu rgyan byas// ser dang gnag dang dkar ba'i zhal// phyag drug pa ni rnam par bsgom// yid bzhin nor bu rdo rje dang // 'khor lo dwe yI g.yas su bsgom// dril bu pad ma ser po dang // ral gri g.yon du bsgom
8b5(rgyud 'grel): par bya// de bzhin thugs ka lngas phyung ste// nga rgyal gnas la gnas pa rnams// yang dag sbyangs nas lho yi 'char// rin po che yi dbus su bzhugs// a ro li ka sngags las skyes pa'i// mtha' yas rdo rje can dbyung ste// zhi ba pad+mararA
8b6(rgyud 'grel): ga'i 'od/ mi bskyed pas ni dbu rgyan byas// mgon po ral pa'i thor tshugs 'chang // dmar dang gnag dang dkar ba'i zhal// sgeg pa'i nyams dang yang dag ldan// phyag drug par ni rnam par bsgom/ g.yon pas dril bu dang
9a1(rgyud 'grel): bcas pa'i// pad ma'i sdong bu 'dzin mdzad cing // pad ma thugs ka'i phyogs gnas pa// g.yas pa yis ni 'byed par mdzad// rdo rje 'khor lo g.yas gnyis kyi// rin chen ral gri g.yon gnyis kyis// sngon bzhin 'dod
9a2(rgyud 'grel): chags can sbyangs nas// rgyab kyi pad+ma la bzhugs pa'o// pradz+nyA d+h+r-ika sngags las sprul pa'i// sngags pas don yod rdo rje can// mgon po sku mdog ljang gu dbyung // thor tshugs cod pan dag gis brgyan// ljang dang gnag dang dkar ba'i zhal// phyag
9a3(rgyud 'grel): drug 'od zer rnam par 'phro// ral gri sna tshogs rdo rje dang // 'khor lo g.yas su bsgom par bya// phyag g.yon rnams na dril bu dang // pad+ma ljang nor bu de bzhin du// log pa'i ngag can sems can rnams// rnam par sbyangs nas slar byon te// de
9a4(rgyud 'grel): bzhin byang gi phyogs su ni// sna tshogs rdo rje dag la bzhugs// zhe sdang gti mug de bzhin chags/ yidade bzhin nor bu dam tshig ste// rigs ni lnga po 'di rnams nyid// 'dod dang thar pA rab bsgrub pa'o// mo ha ra ti'i sngags las skyes// lha mo spyan ni dbyung
9a5(rgyud 'grel): bar bya// dkar zhing zhi ba'i nyams dang ldan// snang mdzad kyis ni spyi bor mtshan// dkar dang gnag dang dmar ba'i zhal// phyag drug par ni rnam par bsgom// 'khor lo rdo rje de bzhin du// ut+pal dkar po g.yas rnams su// dri lA bu de bzhin rin
9a6(rgyud 'grel): chen dang // ral gri g.yon du bsgom par bya// de bzhin thugs ka nas phyung ste// phyogs bcu rnams su gzigs nas ni// gdon dang nad gdung 'jig rten rnams// thugs rje chen pos zhi mdzad ste// slar byon zla ba'i dbus nyid du// shar gyi
9b1(rgyud 'grel): mtshams su bzhugs pa'o// de Sha ra ti'i sngags las byung // lha mo ma ma ki dbyung ste// ut+pal sngon po'i 'dab ltar sngo// bzhin bzang shin tu yid du 'ong // gnag dang dkar dang dmar ba ste// mi bskyed pas ni dbu rgyan byas// rdo rje 'khor lo de bzhin
9b2(rgyud 'grel): du/ ut+pal sngo dmar g.yas rnams na// dril bu rin chen ral gri phyag/ g.yon na bsnams pa phyung nas ni// bgegs chen 'jigs pas gzir ba rnams// thugs rje chen pos bsrung mdzad de// slar ni byon par mdzad nas su// bden
9b3(rgyud 'grel): bral du ni bzhugs pa'o// ra gA ra ti'i sngags las byung // gos dkar mo ni dbyung bya ste// dmar dang gnag dang dkar ba'i zhal// nor bu pad ma rA ga'i 'od// 'od dpag med bcas ral ba'i tshogs// phyag drug par ni rnam par bsgom//
9b4(rgyud 'grel): g.yon pa dril bur bcas pa yI// ud pal sdong bu 'dzin mdzad pa// thugs kar gnas pa'i ud pa la// dmar po g.yas kyis 'byed pa rA mdzad// rdo rje 'khor lo g.yas dag na// nor bu ral gri g.yon dag na// bsnams pa rnam par
9b5(rgyud 'grel): phyung nas ni// nad chen rnam par zhi mdzad de// slar byon pad ma'i dbus nyid du// rlung gi mtshams su bzhugs pa'o// badz+ra ra ti'i sngags las byung // yid 'ong sgrol mA dbyung byas te// ljang dang gnag dang dkar ba'i zhal// ngur ba'i lo ma'i 'od dang mnyaM/
9b6(rgyud 'grel): dran yod pas ni gtsug tor byas// phyag drug par ni rnam par bsgom// sna tshogs rdo rje 'khor lo dang // ud pal sngon po g.yas rnams// dril bu rin chen ral gri ni// brtul zhugs can gyis g.yon du bsam// de bzhin sems can kun dbang
10a1(rgyud 'grel): mdzad pa sna tshogs rdo rje'i gdan la ni// phyung 'di slar yang byon nas su// zhi ba'i gnas su bzhugs pa'o// rim pa gnyis par rnal 'byor pas// gzugs rdo rje la sogs pa dbyung // me yi mtshams su dgod bya ba// lha mo yid 'ong
10a2(rgyud 'grel): gzugs rdo rje// zhal gsum phyag drug dkar ba ste// dbu rgyan rnam par snang mdzad dpal// gnyis kyis me long 'dzin pa ste// lhagra ma gti mug dga' dang mtshungs// bden bral du dgod lha mo ni// sgra yi rdo rje phyag drug ma// zhal gsum
10a3(rgyud 'grel): sku mdog ser mo ste// dbu rgyan rin chen 'byung ldan yin// phyag gnyis pi wang gis 'brel zhing // lhag ma mA ma ki dang mtshungs// rlung gi gnas dgod lha mo ni// dri yi rdo rje phyag drug ma// zhal gsum sku mdog dmar mo ste/ 'od dpag med dang
10a4(rgyud 'grel): thor tshugs 'chang // phyag gnyis kyang ni dung gis 'brel// lhag ma gos dkar mo dang mtshungs// dbang ldan du dgong lha mo ni// ro yi rdo rje phyag drug ma// zhal gsum sku mdog ljang gu ste// dbu rgyan la nI rnga sgra can// phyag gnyis na ni ro yi snod//
10a5(rgyud 'grel): lcug ma sgrol ma'i rnam pa yin// rdo rje sems dpa' legs mkhyud ste/ 'khor lo'i dbus na rnam bzhugs pa'i// reg bya rdo rje bsam bya ste// zhal sogs bdag po lta bu'o// rim pa gsum pa'i shar gyi ni// snam bur brtul zhugs can gyis dbyung
10a6(rgyud 'grel): mo b+h+rUM sa bin las rdzogs pa/ byams pa sa yi snying po dag/ oM gyi sa bon ngag las byung // phyag na rdo rje mkha' snying po// lho yi phyogs kyi snam bu la// sngags pas go rims ji bzhin du// oM dang hUM las yang dag byung // 'jig rten dbang
10b1(rgyud 'grel): phyug 'jam pa'i dbyangs// 'di dag nub tu dbyung bar bya// byang phyogs su yang dbyung ba ni/ oM dang saM gi sa bon skyes// sgrib sel kun tu bzang por bcas// 'di rnams dbu rgyan rang gi mgon// sku mdog la sogs de dang mtshungs// phyag dang mtshon
10b2(rgyud 'grel): cha dag kyang slar// rang gi bdag po rnams dang mtshungs// byams pa 'ba' zhig g.yas pa na// klu shing me tog rnam par bsnams// 'di rnams sems can rnams kyis ni// skye mched rnams ni rnam sbyangs nas// lha yi spyan sogs rtsol ba po// slar
10b3(rgyud 'grel): byon gdan rnams la bzhugs pa'o// ya mAn+ta kr-ita sngags las gyur// sngags pa gshin rje mthar byed dbyung // gnag dang dkar dang dmar ba'i zhal// me 'phro 'thibs po kun nas 'khrigs// dbyug pa rdo rje 'khor lo ni// phyag g.yas rnams na bsnam/
10b4(rgyud 'grel): de bzhin// thugs kar sdigs mdzub zhags pa dang / dril bu dgra sta g.yon rnams na// dbang po la sogs tshogs kyang bcas// mi bzang bgegs rnams skrag mdzad cing // pad ma nyi ma mnyam gnas nas// shar gyi phyogs su bzhugs pa'o//
10b5(rgyud 'grel): pradz+nyAn+ta kr-ita sngags las byung // rin chen 'byung ldan dbu rgyan can// sku mdog dkar zhing sbrul gyis brgyan/ gzhan gyis mi thub sngags pas dbyung // gsus khyim che zhing spyan gsum pa// dkar dang gnag dang dmar ba'i zhal// mche ba gtsigs
10b6(rgyud 'grel): shing rnam par gnyer// me 'phro 'thibs po kun nas 'khrigs// rdo rje dbyug pa ral gri ni// g.yas kyi phyag rnams na bsnams shing kasnying gar sdigs mdzub zhags pa dang // dral bu dgra sta g.yon rnams na// mi bzang bgegs ni skrag pa
11a1(rgyud 'grel): mdzad// g.yon rkyang ba yi gom stabs kyis// pad ma nyi ma mnan nas ni// gshin rje'i phyogs su de bzhugaso// pad mAn+ta kr-ita sngags las byung // rta mgrin sngags pas dbyung bar bya// spyan gsum prad ma ra ga'i
11a2(rgyud 'grel): dmar dang gnag dang dkar ba'i zhal// zhal rtsub gsus khyim che ba dang // 'od dpag med pa'i cod pan can/ dpa' bo g.yon rkyang ba yi sa gnas// me 'bar tshogs ni rnam par 'khrug/ pad ma ral gr-i gtun shing ni// g.ya
11a3(rgyud 'grel): kyi phyag rnams na bsnams shing // snyems pa dang bcas dril bu dang // dgra sta zhags pa g.yon rnams na// pad ma nyi ma lA gnas te// phyogs bcu dag tu gzigs nas ni// klu rnams skrag par mdzad nas su// chu bdag phyogs
11a4(rgyud 'grel): su bzhugs pa'o// big+h+nAn+ta kr-ita sngags las byung // rnga sgra yi ni cod pan can// ut+pal sngon po'i 'dab ltar ljang // bdud rtsi thabs sbyor dbyung bar bya// sngo dang dkar dang dmar ba'i zhal// zhal gdungs pa yi rnam par 'gyur// gsum
11a5(rgyud 'grel): khyim che zhing spyan gsum pa// dmar po 'bar bas rnam par brgyan// sna tshogs rdo rje 'khor lo dang // gtun shing yang ni g.yas rnams na// de bzhin sdigs mdzub zhags pra dang / dril bu dgra sta g.yon na bsnams// bgegs rnams
11a6(rgyud 'grel): skrag par mdzod nas su// g.yon brkyang ba yi gom pa'i stabs// pad ma nyi mar mnyam gtsugs nas// lus ngan phyogasu bzhugs pa'o// rang sngags yi ge las byung ba// mi g.yo ba yang dbyung bar bya// spyan gsum in+d+ra nI la'i mdog/
11b1(rgyud 'grel): dbu brgyan rnam par snang mdzad dpal ka/ mche ba rnam par gtsigs pa'i zhal// gnag dang dkar dang dar ba'i zhal// mi bzang ha ha zhes pa'ang sgra// gsus khyim che zhing stobs po che// ral gri rdo rje 'khor lo ni// g.yas kyi phyag rnams ma
11b2(rgyud 'grel): bsnams shing // sdigs mdzub dang ni sgra sta dang // zhags pa g.yon gyi phyag rnams na// bgegs dang rims sogs bcom nas ni// g.yon brkyang ba yi gom pa'i stabs// pad ma nyi mar mnyam btsugs nas// me lha'i phyogasu de bzhug so//
11b3(rgyud 'grel): rang sngags yi ge las rdzogs pa// brtul zhugs can gyi 'dod rgyal dbyung // dpa' bo in+d+ra nI la'i 'od// rin chen 'byung ldan dbu rgyan can// gnag dang dkar dang dmar ba'i zhal// gsus khyim che zhing 'jigs su rung // phyag gnyis rdo rje
11b4(rgyud 'grel): hUM mdzad kyi// phyag rgya dag ni 'chang bar mdzad// rdo rje ral gri g.yas ngag gis// g.yon pa zhags pa lcags kyu'o// bgegs 'jigs byed pa bden bral du kA g.yon brkyang ba yi nyi mar bzhugs// rang sngags yi ge las byung ba// brtul
11b5(rgyud 'grel): zhugs can gyis dbyug sngon dbyung // spyan gsum sprin sngon lta bu ste// 'od dpag med pa'i dbu rgyan can// sngo dang dkar dang dra ma rA ba'i zhal// gsus khyim che zhing 'jigs pa bskyed// dbyug pA ral gri 'khor lo ni// g.yas kyi phyag
11b6(rgyud 'grel): rnams na bsnams shing // snying gar sdigs mdzub zhags pa dang // pad ma dgra sta g.yon rnams na// yams dang 'tshe ba'i 'jigs bsal nas// g.yon brkyang gom stabs gnas pa yis// pad ma nyi mar mnyam btsugs te//
12a1(rgyud 'grel): rlung lha'i phyogs su bzhugs pa'o ka rlung sngags yi ge las byung ba// d+hA s+thA li ni dbu rgyun can// stobs po nA ni sngags byas dbyung // At+pal sngon po'i 'dab 'dra'i 'od// gnag dang dkar dang dmar pa'i zhal/ spyan
12a2(rgyud 'grel): gsum 'jigs pa'i sgra drang ldan// yan lag thams cad sbrul gyis brgyan/ gsus khyim che zhing 'jigs su rlung // dbyug pa ral gri 'khor lo ni ka g.yas kyi phyag rnams na bsnams shing // snying gar sdigs mdzub zhags pa dang // pad ma
12a3(rgyud 'grel): dgra sta g.yon rnams ni// mkha' 'gro la sogs 'jigs pa 'joms// g.yon brkyang goms pa'i stabs kyis te// pad ma nyi mar mnyam btsugs nas// dbang ldan phyogs su bzhugs pa'o// rang sngags yi ge lasna byung ba'i// gtsug
12a4(rgyud 'grel): tor 'khor los bsgyur ba dbyung // mkha' ltar sngo sangs drag po ni// mi bskyod bya yi dbu rgyun byas// gnag dang dkar dang du maR+sha ba'i zhal// gtso bo spyan gsum gsus pa 'byung // g.yas dang g.yon gyi phyag gnyis kyi// spyi bor gtsug
12a5(rgyud 'grel): taur 'dzin mdzad cing // rdo rje pad ma gla las dag gis// sdigs mdzub ral gri g.yon dag gis// 'tsho ba thams cad rnam 'jig cing // g.yon brkyang goms stabs snyems po yis// pad ma nyi mar mnyam gnas nas// tshangs pa'i gnas
12a6(rgyud 'grel): su de bzhugs// rab sngags yi ge las rdzogs pa// gnod mdzes rgyal po sngags pas dbyung // spyan gsum na mkha' bzang po'i 'od// gnas dang dkar dang dmar paba'i zhal// gsus khyim che zhing gtsigs pa'i zha la// mi bskyod
12b1(rgyud 'grel): pas ni dbu brgyan byas// rdo rje 'khor lo rin chen ni// g.yas pa'i phyag rnams na 'dzin cing // / snying gar sdigs mdzub zhugs pa dang // pad ma ral gri g.yon rnams na// brtan pa dang ni g.yo ba'i dug/ kA la ku Ta la sogs kun// bcom
12b2(rgyud 'grel): nas bgegs kyi bdag po ni// thams cad kun tu zhi mdzad nas// ma lus bka' ni rdzogs byas te// g.yon brkyang goms stabs gnas pa yis// pad ma nyi mar mnyam gnas te// sa yi 'og tu de bzhugs so// lha ni sum cu gnyis
12b3(rgyud 'grel): rang bzhin/ dkyil 'khor thams cad phyung nas ni// 'khor lo'i dbus su gnas gyur nas// de nas phra mo'i rnal 'byor brtsam// sna yi rtse mor nyungs kar bsam// nyung kar rgyu dang mi rgyu ba// ye shes gnas ni nyams dga' ba// gas/
12b4(rgyud 'grel): ba'i ye shes brtags pa bsgom// rin chen chen po kha dog lnga// nyungs kar gyi ni 'bru tshad tsam// sna yi rtse mor nan tan du// rnal 'byor gyis ni rtag tu bsgom// rin chen brtan par gyur na spro// brtan par ma gyur yong mi spro// sangs rgyas
12b5(rgyud 'grel): 'bar ba mnyam pa'i 'od// rab mchog sprin rnams spro bar bya// slong mo za zhing mi bzlas te// bsrungs la dga' bar yang mi bya/ 'dod pa kun la longs spyod cing // sngags kyi yan lag dbyer med bzlas// brjod nas rdo rje spro bya zhing //
12b6(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs nas rab tu bsdu bar bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// don dam pa yi bzlas par gsungs// phra mo'i rnal 'byor bzlas pa yang // rnam gnyis ci 'dod byas nas su// slar yang sngags pas bdag nyid ni// de bzhin nyid la gzhug
13a1(rgyud 'grel): par bya// de nas dkyil 'khor gnas lha ma// gan yis bdag po ma mthong nas// tshigs su brjod pa 'dri ba ni mos// bdang chen pos par byed// sems can khams ni gnas kyi dbang phyug khyod ni
13a2(rgyud 'grel): thugs// dga' ba yid 'ong don chen 'dod pas bdag la skyabasu gsol// mgon pos gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na// sems can yab gnyen mchog chen bdag la dgyes par mdzad du gsol// rdo rje'i sku khyod bka
13a3(rgyud 'grel): 'khor lo sems nAnA mang por phan// sangs rgyas rnams don byang chub mchog don panA ba rjes bstan pa// mgon pos gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na// chags pas 'dod chags dam tshig bdag la dgyes par mdzad du
13a4(rgyud 'grel): gsol// khyod ni rdo rje'i gsung ste kun la phan zhing thugs brtse ba// 'jig rten dag gis dgos pa'i don mdzad pa la rta ga tu brtson// mgon pos gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na// rab dga'i spyod pas kun tu
13a5(rgyud 'grel): bzang po bdag la dgyes par mdzod// khyod ni rdo rje'i 'dod pa dam tshig mchog gi phan don che// rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi gdung mchog mnyam nyid rjes su thugs brtse ba// mgon pos gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na//
13a6(rgyud 'grel): yon tan rin chen mang po'i gter gyur bdag la dgyes par mdzod// de ltar yang dag yon tan ni// brjod pas bslang ba'i mgon po la// mi bskyod la sogs ngo bo yi// de bzhin gshegs rnams bstod par mdzad// mi bskyod rdo rje
13b1(rgyud 'grel): ye shes che// rdo rje dbyings ni mkhas pa che// rdo rje gsum mchog dkyil 'khor gsum// gsang ba gsung khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rnam par snang mdzod dag pa che// rdo rje zhi ba dga' ba che// rang bzhin 'od gsal chos rnams ni// ston mdzad rdo rje/
13b2(rgyud 'grel): khyod phyag la Shin chen rgyal po rab tu zab// rdo rje na mkha' dri med mkha'// rang bzhin dag pa gos pa med// gsang ba gsungs shig khyod phyag 'tshal// rdo rje dpag med rgyal po che// mi rtog na mkha' rdo rje can// 'dod chags pha rol phyin pa
13b3(rgyud 'grel): bsnyes// rdo rje gsung khyod phyag 'tsha lo// don yod rdo rje rdzogs sangs rgyas// bsam pa thams cad longs rdzogs mdzad// dag pa ngo bo nyid las byung // rdo rje sems dpa' khyod phyag 'tshal// sangs rgyas kyis bstod de nas 'khor lo
13b4(rgyud 'grel): mnyes mdzad ste// gsang ba mchog ni ji lta ji bzhin rab gsal byas// rang gi lus kyi 'khor lo lnga ni 'khor lo gzhug/ mgon po bde ba chen po gcig pu bzhugs par gyur// de ltar rnal 'byor bzhi byed rnal 'byor pas// hUM yig
13b5(rgyud 'grel): snying por 'jig rten rab tu bsgom// de byung 'gro ba rdo rje snyems dpar blta// langs nas de'i blos ji bzhin dpyad par bya// sngags pa ting 'dzin la dmigs pas// gang tshe lus ni skam gyur nA// lus ngag yid ni tshim byed pa'i// sbyor
13b6(rgyud 'grel): ba 'di ni bsgom par bya// mtho gang tsam gyis spags par ni// mgo bor dkyil 'khor brtag par bya// oM yig dbus su gnas bsam nas// bdud rtsi lnga po dbab par bya// rdo rje sbyor ba 'di yis ni// skad cig gis ni gzi can 'gyur//

15b2(rgyud 'grel): phyag 'tshal// rgyud kyi rgyal po gsang 'dus kyi// rdzogs rims don bsdus rim bzhin bshang// bla ma'i zhal gyi bdud rtsi 'di// phyi don drug tu shes par bya// dbang po/ bskyed byag/ gzhi'i gnas lugs sa zung ban bstan// ga nyis pa
15b3(rgyud 'grel): 'khor bar 'khrul lugs bstan// gsum pa sbyang gzhi'i gnas thabs bstan// bzhi pa lam gyi rim lnga bstan// lnga pa 'bras bu'i thob se'u dang po da / rgyud bye tsa'i do/ tshul bstan// drug pa phan yon bstan pa'o// dang po gzhi'i gnas lugs
15b4(rgyud 'grel): ni/ gzhi yis 'bras bu byed pa yin/ sems can rnas de/ sangs rgyas spyod bsdus na snrums su blang babs mnyam ngo bo nyid sde pa dad med pa swA gsus med mnyam// gzong nasA zhi zhing ma skyes pa/ thong ba skyed pa de la 'khor rang bzhin lhun grub de dang mya 'das
15b5(rgyud 'grel): med// rang las gsum gyi mabar bzhin mya dran 'das pa de// gdong nas rang la gnas pa yin// gzhi dang rang bzhin rgyu yin te/ lam ni thabs zhes bya ba tshas tshad yin// de bzhini mi 'phrogs 'bra sa de pa gnyis med sa bu yin// thog ma tha ma med
15b6(rgyud 'grel): bdag ma pa nyid kyi byed zhig/ 'ad chos kyis rnam par stong grol med pa ma papa nyid mi 'gyur sde me nga / mtshan ma med/ mi 'jigs sde ba myed klu myin// des gsol du med pas nyid gas pa sa ma bya gsus nyi ti

16a2(rgyud 'grel): lta bur 'pho 'gyur med/ skye bgag med pas mthar chos sgra gnyis pa 'od gas so ba sems can rnams ni sangs rgyas nyid dbyir med skragasum ngo bo rang bzhin yang 'di nye bar zhibs te rang bzhin gyis mtshan ma mi dmigs pa 'odags pa 'gro kun snying po yongs la 'khrul lugs

16a4(rgyud 'grel): snang 'khrul/ 'khor ba thog ma med rgyud phyi ma nas pa nas// rlung drung sems sems rang bzhin lusu bsags 'khor// 'khrul ge rgya 'dzin pa'i rdo rje rab tu gang dag dang chos kyi gang rdzob kyi nyid zil gsungs// de la sems nyid do rang bzhin stong ba bo de//

16b1(rgyud 'grel): ba'i rlung sems ma rig 'khrul// de las kun rdzob las sgrib byung // rlung sems mi shigs thig lnga ste// snang stong ngo po dag par gnas// lus ngag sems dang sgyu mar sbyor// 'od gsal mthong dang zung 'jug bsgom// rlung sems dri ma zad pa na//
16b2(rgyud 'grel): mya ngan stong zhing ma 'khrul pas 'das pas rmilas rgyam lta bur thig le 'dras sa byas kyi rang bzhin ngag/ thig le ma rtogs rnam shes rlung // rnal 'byor pas lam ru dben pa gsum bskyong pus ma rig phyi gnyis med yul shar// ga cag lnga'i zung yul dkar
16b3(rgyud 'grel): dmar sna tshogs zhe na/ nang du shes bya 'dzin par skyes// bye ba gzung 'dzin gnyis la rlung sems dag pa skye ba gcig ltos pas// bag chags lus nyon 'khor ba rgyas// gzung 'dzin mi bden bzhin du kun rdzob snang // tshogs drug rnam pa phyi'i snod
16b4(rgyud 'grel): kyi 'jig rten kyang // 'byung bzhi la so tshogs drug nang du bdag rung gas sna bdag dang bdag ging tshogs snang // nang gi bcud kyi sems can kyang // 'gro las dang drug skye rga na 'chir snang // 'dus byas yang mi ba'i chos skye dang tha skar gnas dang 'jig pa dang rlung gis
16b5(rgyud 'grel): srid pa bar mar gnas pa dang / de las skye ba len pa yang // mngal skyes sgong skyes drod rgyus skyes// de la ma las skyes pa yang // rlung gis bar ngo'i shes pa rlung dang bcas/ pho mo'i 'du 'phro sa bon gnyis// sno bcud thams cad rlung gis rten 'brel tsam rnam shwe

17a2(rgyud 'grel): de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la ni// chos/ gnas skabs lnga rgya 'tshogs pas 'chi ba'i chos chu me rlung na mkhar thim nyid ya shes thugs rjer gnas/ rgyud phyi ma nas dang po skyes 'dod 'dun gnod sems gnyid rmugs sgong 'gyod the tshom gnas 'khor ba nA// tha ma thams cad kyi mra
17a3(rgyud 'grel): mkhyen pa'i bar// lus dang ngag chos sku gzugs sku gnyis sems spros dang bral// 'od gsal zung 'jug rab bzhin rnam pa pa mkhyen zer gnas// de las kun rdzob lus 'di la// rtsa rnams brten nas gnas pa yin// rtsa yi nang du thig le brten// thig le

22b4(rgyud 'grel): mongs sreg/ gsum pa sgyu lus bslabs pa ni// sa mtshams rnam pa lngar shes bya/ dang po rang bzhin sgyu mar bstan// gnyis pa sgyu lus dpe la sbyar// gsum pa dpe don sbyar la bsgom// bzhi pa de nyid bsgom par bya// lnga pa

23b2(rgyud 'grel): nyid grol// dngos dgra kun las rnam par grol// gzugs sgra la sogs sgyu mar spyod// sgyu ma'i ting 'dzin brtag pa na// ngan song mi 'gro sdug bsngal zhig/ nyon mongs rags pa chu bri nas// 'od gsal bden pa mthong bar
23b3(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur// sgyu lus nyin par sbyang thabs so// da ni mtshan mo'i sgyu lus sbyangs// mtshon mo 'i rmi lam sgyu lus bzung // de la bdun pa drag po bya// rmi lam na na chos rnams kun// rmi lam 'khrul pa sgyu mar bsgom// de la spro/

28b1(rgyud 'grel): dag pas 'od gsal dag/ sku dang gsung thugs mkha' mnyam dag/ nyon mongs las rnams grol ba yi// spangs thob rtag chad skye 'gag med// yod med gnyis ka gnyis med min// 'khor 'das gnyis mod dmigs spros shong //

28b3(rgyud 'grel): bden pa gnyis kyi tshul la gnas// de nyid gnyis med ye shes te// chos nyid smra bsdam brjod las 'das// 'di la bsam du ci yang med// thams cad stong pa'i chos nyid la// bstan par bya ba cung zad med// lam
28b4(rgyud 'grel): gyi chos rnams zad pas te// slar zhing gang la'ang mi slob bo// blang dor med cing sangs rgyas med// chos kyi sku zhes ming du brjod// thams cad mkhyen pa'i sangs rgyas yin// da ni 'bras bu'i thob tshul bstan// mi gnas mya
28b5(rgyud 'grel): ngan 'das pa de// chos dbyings skye ba med pa'i dbyings// rdo rje lta bu'i ting 'dzin gyis// sangs rgyas byang chub ye shes 'di // gnyis med rnam dag ye shes sku// dbyings dang ye shes gnyis su med// dag pa gnyis
28b6(rgyud 'grel): med ye shes sku// sku ni mi 'gyur ma skyes pa// gsung dang thugs kyang mtshan ma med// sangs rgyas rnams ni chos skur bzhugs// de'i rnam 'phrul gzugs sku gnyis// chos nyid 'grib pa med par dag/ nam mkha' lta bur
29a1(rgyud 'grel): 'pho 'gyur med// chos sku skye med sku de ni// gnyis med ye shes ston pa rnams// sangs rgyas rnams la chos sku de// nam mkha' khyab par gnas pa yin// chos nyid rnam par dag pa la// bzhengs dang
29a2(rgyud 'grel): bzhugs pa mi mnga' yang // chos sku nam mkha' lta bu la// longs sku sprin gzha' lta bu de/ longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku ru snang // mtshan bzang sum cu rtsa gnyis dang // dpe byad bzang po brgyad cur ldan// longs sku rdo
29a3(rgyud 'grel): rje 'chang ba de// chus nyid rnam par dag pa la// bzhangs dang bzhugs pa ma mnga' yang // thugs rje chen po dri med dang // sngon gyi smon lam stobs dag gis// gdul bya byang chub sems dpa' la// longs sku gzha'
29a4(rgyud 'grel): tshochen sgyu bu de// stong gsum khyab par gnas nas su// 'og min chos kyi pho brang du// rdo rje 'chang gri rnam pa nges// 'khor ba ma stongs par du ni/ rgyun mi 'chad pa'i chos gsungs so// longs sgra de yi 'phrin las las//
29a5(rgyud 'grel): dang po briskyong rnams bsgom pa yis// 'bras bu longs su mtshan rnams rgyus// dbang po rdzogs rims bstan pa las// 'bras bu ye shes chos sgro thob// drug pa phan yon bstan pa ni// sring po tha ma dbang po rlab/ zung
29a6(rgyud 'grel): 'jug skye meng rtogs pa na// kun spyod spyad pas shes sgrib spangs/ mi slob thung 'jug rtogs gyur nas// tshe 'di nyid la sangs rgya'o// dper na sbrul gyi shun brjes ltar// skye ba gcig la mchog 'grub yin// tshe 'dir ma
29b1(rgyud 'grel): par gzhag pa la// ngag dpon sems dpon sgyu lus bsgom// mnyam byar gzhag pa'i dus nyid du// 'od gasngal mthong la ma goms na// rnal 'byor pa de g.yengs pas khyer// sgom dang spyod pa ma khom pas// nam zhig 'chi ba'i dus nyid du/
29b2(rgyud 'grel): snang gsum lugs su 'jug pa dang // phung po khams dang skye mched sogs// rnam shes rlung dang bcas pa thim// phyi dbugs chad de nang dbugs gnas/ sngar gyi sgom pa'i 'od gsal dang // shi ba stong pa'i 'od gsal gnyis// chu la
29b3(rgyud 'grel): chu bzhin gnyis med 'dres// bar dor 'od gsal skye med rtogs/ bar dor sgyu ma dag pa langs// gzha' tshon lta bu'i ye shes sku// zung du 'jug pa de langs nas// bar do'i yul lnga stong par bsgom/ 'dzam bu gling ni phrag brgya ru//
29b4(rgyud 'grel): sprul pa bye ba phrag brgya yis// gdul bya gang mos bsam pa la// de dang 'thun pa'i chos ston no// sku gsum ngon dam ro gcig yin// kun rdzob tsam du sangs rgyas de// chos kyi dbyings kyi pho brang du// ji ltar mkhyen pa'i ye shes la// gang
29b5(rgyud 'grel): gi rlung gi sangs rgyas dang // byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis bskor// 'phrin las sprul sku sgyu 'dra las// ji snyed pa yi ye shes kyis// kun la khyab cing sprul pa 'gyed// gdul bya dag pa gzhan snang la// 'khor dang myang 'das mkhyen bzhin
29b6(rgyud 'grel): dud/ de yi chos kyi gos mi 'gyur// dper na 'das kyi pad+ma bzhin// chos kyi dbyings las ma g.yos so// dper na yid bzhin nor bu bzhin// 'bad pa med par 'gro ba 'dren// ye shes sprul sku longs sgyu rnams// chos kyi sku la brten nas su// chos
30a1(rgyud 'grel): gang la'ang mo gnas so// mthar thug pa la brjod du song // bar dor zung 'jug mi slob thob// bar dor rdzogs par sangs rgya'o// cha 'dor smra lus rtogs pa na// nam zhig 'chi ba'i dus nyid du// snang gsum
30a2(rgyud 'grel): ngag gis lugs su 'jug/ 'chi ba shes rab pha rol phyin// 'dun pa drag pos rjes dran bya// phung khams skye mched yul dbang 'dus// snang gsum 'ong gsal rtogs na rab/ 'od gsal rtogs par ma gyur na// tshe 'dir
30a3(rgyud 'grel): sgyu lus bsgom pa de/ bar dor sgyu lus ngos zin te/ bar dor sgyu lus 'od gsal sbyangs// gal te skye bA lan na yang // rAng dbang yod pas lus len no// 'gro ba'i don byed chos sgrub lus/ de ltar bu ru lus blangs la//
30a4(rgyud 'grel): 'gro don byas la mchog sgrubs pas// mngon par byang chub thob 'gyur ro// skye ba brgyud pa'i sangs rgyas yin// de ltar rab kyis tshe 'di thob/ 'bring ni bar dor 'grub pa las/ tha mi skye ba brgyud nas thob// dpal gsang
30a5(rgyud 'grel): ba 'dres pa'i man ngag kha che'i paN+Di ta na ro pas mdzad pa rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po rig pa brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor pa// dpal

30b2(rgyud 'grel): dan po pas mdzad pa'i rim pa sdu bsdus pa gsal mar ba chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ rgya gar skad du/ bany+tsa kra mU saM kra h+ya pra b+ha wA/ bod skad du/ rim pa lnga bsdus pa gsal ba// dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la phyag
30b3(rgyud 'grel): 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba che// rim pa lnga la gnas pa'o// dngos po'i gnas su lam dang ni// 'bras bu skye ba'i rim pa'o// dngos po'i gnas lugs gnyis yin te// sems dang lus kyi gnas thabs las//
30b4(rgyud 'grel): rags dang pA dang shin tu pra/ thun mongs dbyer med rim zhes bya// gnyid dang rmi lam snyoms 'jug pa// tha mal dus dang rnam pa bzhi// 'khor lo bzhi yi bdag nyid kyis// rtse dang thig le sems zhes pa// lus dang dus dang yul gyi ni/

30b6(rgyud 'grel): dben sngags dang sems gsum gyi// sgyu ma mngon par byang chub pa// zung 'jug rim pa shes par 'gyur// sngags kyis yi ge'i 'khor lo ni// dang por chu skyes 'dab brgyad pa// phyi nang gsang ba'i tshul gyis ni// rim pa ldan par
31a1(rgyud 'grel): bsam gtan bya// phyi rim shes rab dbyangs yig mtshan// bar ma gsal byed thabs bcas pa// gnyis su med par nang mar gnas// phyogs mtshams rim par ting nge 'dzin// sbyor ba rnam pa gsum
31a2(rgyud 'grel): rang bzhin// dbus su mig gi thig le te/ a dang bcas pa srog gyur gang // kun gyi snying po spro zhing sdung // 'byung ba bzhi yi rlung rnams nyid// rlung dang sngags su rab sbyor bas// rdo rje bzlas pa sbyang bar bya// 'byung 'jug
31a3(rgyud 'grel): gnas pa nyid du bshad // tha mal rnam rtog bag chags rnams// sngags nyid sems su dmigs pas so// lus dag pas ni rtog pa dag/ rlung dag pas ni dri med 'gyur// rlung dag pas ni ye shes kyi// kun rdzob sgyu ma mngon du
31a4(rgyud 'grel): byed// de nyid mngon par byang chub pas// zung 'jug ye shes thob par 'gyur// las rnams bya ba 'phrin las tshogs// rnam shos ye shes sbyor bas 'grub// rtogs rnams rim par 'char ba'i dngos// ye shes lnga yis
31a5(rgyud 'grel): rgyu mthun nyams// gsal snang 'bar ba'i ngang du'o// yan lag rlung las mngon shes thob// rtog pa'i tshogs ni mar 'grib cing // gnyen po ye shes yar 'phel tu// ye shes rim pa rang las rnyed // gcig dang du mer
31a6(rgyud 'grel): dmigs mi phyed// dang po smi gi rgyu lta bu'i nyams// 'od zer lnga dang bcas pa 'char// gnyis pa zla ba lta bu dang // gsum pa nyi ma'i 'od kyi 'khrig/ mtshams snang las ni thob pa ste// mtshams bral dus kyi ye shes che// mngon
31b1(rgyud 'grel): par byang chub tshul gnas pas// dri med ye shes mngon par rdzogs// rtags dang rtags can 'char tshul ni// ye shes 'bar dang rdzogs pa'i dus// rlung sems tsam lngas byung ba yis// sgyu ma'i lus ni snang bar bcas// 'od gsal
31b2(rgyud 'grel): rgyun gyi bsam gtan gyis// las dang sgrib pa bag chags sbyangs// sa la ma rtags kyi rim pa'i tshogs// 'di nyid thob pa'i myur du 'char// nam mkha' dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor bas
31b3(rgyud 'grel): bsam par bya// 'dab ma brgyad pa'i sa bon la// dbus su srog gis sa bon te// yi ge ka nas ha yi bar// k+Sha ni spangs pa'i bzhi bcas pa// dbyangs ni phyi rim snang ba ste// gsal byed par ma mched pa nyid// ma ning snang ba
31b4(rgyud 'grel): thob par brjod// bcu gnyis yig gis thig ler bcas// 'phreng ba lta bur gnas pa ni/ rim pa lnga ldan bsam par bya// 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs pa// oM waM thabs dang shes rab las// sdud cing
31b5(rgyud 'grel): spro bar mdzad pa yi// a zhes dbus su gnas par mdzad// mnyam pa nyid du sems bsdam ste// mnyam bzhag 'khor lo'i lte ba lI// ye shes mnyam par mthong 'gyur ba// nye bar thob pa stong pa che// 'od gsal
31b6(rgyud 'grel): pa yi gnas thob pa// 'khor ba las ni brgal bar 'gyur// thun gcig yang ni nyin gcig gam// zla phyed zla ba lo yi dus// bskal pa 'am bskal pa stong du yang // skad cig re rer gnas pa ni// ye shes sbyor ba rtab du
32a1(rgyud 'grel): 'byung te/ rim pa gnyis pa la gnyis pa// mnyam par zung 'brel nyid bsgom pa// bskyed pa'i rim 'di lha yi sku// rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi dkyil 'khor mchog/ rnam pa mngon du byed pa gang // legs par
32a2(rgyud 'grel): bslab pas mthar phyin 'gyur// lus dben snang ba sems dang lus// rgyu dang mi rgyu 'jig rten bcas// rim pas lha yi bdag nyid sbyar// rdo rje 'chang chen lam du byed// mos pa las byung ting nge 'dzin// rten cing 'brel par 'gyung
32a3(rgyud 'grel): ba'o// rlung gi 'byung 'jug gnas pa gsum// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje lngas// rlung sngags mnyam par rab sbyor grang // rdo rje bzlas pa'i rim pa'o// gsang sngags las byung rnam par shes// snang ba gsum gyi
32a4(rgyud 'grel): bdag nyid ni// ye shis 'jug ldog nges pa gang / sems la dmigs pa'i rim pa'o// rmi lam lus ni rnam sbyangs phyir/ sgyu mar mtshon pa'i dus gang lags// yul snang kun rdzob gang byung ba/ sgyu ma ltar bu'i
32a5(rgyud 'grel): rim pa'o// de bzhin shes pa bsams gtan las// thabs las ma bskyed ting nge 'dzin// rang gsal ngo bo mi rtog pa// 'od gsal don dam rim pa'o// bsam gtan med sbyangs lha yi sku// rang byung ye shes dag pa'i lus
32a6(rgyud 'grel): sbyang gzhi sbyong byed bral bar gnas// zung du 'jug pa'i rim pa'o// byang chub sems ldan bla ma dang / lhag pa'i lha yi rnal 'byor dang // shin tu rnal 'byor rnal 'byor che// rjes su rnal 'byor bcas pa dag/ ting 'dzin rim pa
32b1(rgyud 'grel): ldan pa yis// bstan pa nyer bsgrub pa che// sgrub pa'i ngo bo khyad par du// so sor spyad dang bsam gtan dang // srog rtsol de bzhin 'dzin pa dang // rjes su dran dang ting nge 'dzin// yan lag drug ldan khyad par ro// rim pa bzhi ldan phyag
32b2(rgyud 'grel): rgyar bcas// dbang bzhi sgra bzhi rang 'byung bas// mngon par byang chub tshul lnga las// bskyed dang bskyed cing gnas pa dang // lam gyur rim pa lnga ldan las// byang chub phyogs chos mdo don dang // sbas pa rnam gsum mthar thug
32b3(rgyud 'grel): bcas/ sna tshogs sgra ni mtshon pa'o// gtum mo'i rnal 'byor rlung gis te/ bde chen sems la dmigs pa'o// rmi lam sgyu ma gcig tu sbyangs// bar do rnam gsum bsre ba nyid// nyon mongs ye shes lam ru 'gyur// ldum
32b4(rgyud 'grel): gyur gcod pa 'pho ba ste// grong du 'jug pa yan lag go/ 'od gsal gnas thob mngon sangs rgyas// brtson 'grus can ni tshe 'di nyid// le lo can ni 'chi khA ste// tha ma srid pa'i bar ma dor// mchog thob skus ni gzhan don byed//
32b5(rgyud 'grel): ngo bo rgyu tshul 'byung ba khams// las dang ngo bo dbye ba de nyid rlung // 'byung 'jug gnas pa rnam par brtags// 'bru gsum sngags kyi ngo bo nyid// A li kA li sbyor dbus las// brtags pa grang ldan bzlas pa nyid// sbyor
32b6(rgyud 'grel): dang khyad par thabs ldan las// ngag dbyen rlung gi rnal 'byor bstan// rgyu dang 'bras bu sbyor ba gang // snang ba gsum gyi 'char tshul te// dus dang 'byung 'gyur thabs khyod par// dbyer med ye shes gnas thob pa// spyod pa ye shes
33a1(rgyud 'grel): mngon du byed/ slob dang mi slob der spyod pa'o// rang bzhin shes pa'i lam gyur pa/ rnam shes rgyu mar mtshon pa'i chos// khyad par las dang spyod pa gang // dngos

35a2(rgyud 'grel): nyunying ni de'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro// brjod ma thag pa'i khyad par gnyis pos ni 'di gsal ba'i rang bzhin du ston par byed do// dag pa ni yongs su dag pa'i ye shes kyi rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir/ zhi ba ni nyon

35a6(rgyud 'grel): phyug la sogs pa rnams kyis don mdzad pa'i phyir ro// 'dis ni longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i rang bzhin nyid brjod pa yin no// khyab pa ni rdzogs par longs spyod pa'i sgrar bskyed pa'i sprul pa'i sku mtha' yas pa'i rang
35b1(rgyud 'grel): bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro// 'dis ni sprul pa'i sku'i rang bzhin du brjod par byed do// mtshan ma med pa ni 'od gsal ba la zhugs pa las/ bag chags kyi mtshan nyid kyi mtshan ma nub pa na sngon byas pa'i smon lam gyis ldang
35b2(rgyud 'grel): ba'i phyir ro// de lta bur gyur pa'i bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ da nI sgrub thabs kyi skabs dbye bar gsungs pa ni dpal ldan zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o// dpal ldan 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi sgrub thabs mdor byas
35b3(rgyud 'grel): rim pa zhes bya ba bdag gis brjod ces 'brel to// sems can thams cad kyi phrin pa 'dir skye ba zhes byas pas so// sgrub thabs du ma yod pa nyid yin pa des na/ 'dis ci bye sgyum na/ mtha'i drug don ni rtogs pa ste/
35b4(rgyud 'grel): zhes gsungs pa ste/ mtha' drug ni bshad pa'i khyad par ste/ ldem por dgongs te bshad pa dang / ldem por dgongs pa ma yin pas bshad pa dang / sgra ji bzhin pa dang / sgra ci bzhin ma yin pa dang / nges pa dang drang
35b5(rgyud 'grel): ba'i don gyi rang bzhin don gang la yod pa de ni de skad ces bya ste/ de rtogs pa las te yongs su shes pa las bdag gis brjod dgos pa ni/ kho bo cag gis mtha' drug bshad par rgyu bshad par bya ba yin pa des na
35b6(rgyud 'grel): rgyud la 'jug pa'i don du sgrub thabs byed pa yin no// sgrub thabs gzhan ni rgyud la 'jug pa'i thabasu gyur pa ma yin no zhes bya ba 'di yin no// dgod pa med pa rtogs pa dang ldan pa 'jog pa med pa ma yin nam/ nges
36a1(rgyud 'grel): mdor byas pa'i rim pa bsgom pa las gos pa ci yang snyam bya'i dogs pa bsu nas/ dgos pa ston pa'i lhur len+d+ra pa'i tshogs su bcas pa gnyis gsungs pa ni rnam rtog zhes bya ba la sog

50a3(rgyud 'grel): da ni rdo rje dang pad+ma yongs su sbyong ba brjod pa ni/ sngags pas zhes bya ba la sogs pa nas bzung ste/ de 'og bsgrub pa brtsam par bya ba zhes bya ba'i mthar thug pas so// hUM yig mthon mthing gyis rang gi mtshan ma rdo rje rtse lnga
